***минный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:минный.html>ми́нный</a> (11223)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минный.html>ми́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mínnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mine</li></ol>

***миновать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:миновать.html>минова́ть</a> (2833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">миновати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">minovati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*minovati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миновать.html>минова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">minovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:миновать.html>минова́ть</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>мину́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pass, to elapse <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to go by, to go past <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">without any affect</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:миновать.html>минова́ть</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Čemú bytʹ, tovó ne <b>minovátʹ</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What must be, must be; What happens, happens.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial or dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn (an age)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миновать.html>минова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">minovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to evade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to end, to finish</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неминуемый.html>немину́емый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neminújemyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">немину́чий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neminúčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разминуться.html>размину́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razminútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***миномет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:миномет.html>миномёт</a> (8959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мёт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mjót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миномет.html>миномёт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">minomjót</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миномет.html>миномёта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миномет.html>миномёты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миномет.html>миномётов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rocket launcher</li>
<li>mortar, trench mortar</li>
<li>torpedo tube</li></ol>

***минус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нус</a> (15661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mínus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нуса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нусы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нусов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>minus</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> minus sign, −</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> disadvantage, defect, shortcoming
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плюс.html>плю́сы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нусы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pljúsy i mínusy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pros and cons</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a subzero temperature (below zero degrees Celsius)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  Михаил Задоронов (Mikhail Zadoronov),  <cite>Задорнов €нд <a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>Ко</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лице</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стои́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:минус.html>ми́нус</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na úlice stoít <b>mínus</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Outside it’s below freezing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***минуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>мину́ть</a> (7181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*minǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>мину́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">minútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миновать.html>минова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pass, to elapse <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">(of time) to pass or move by</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to go by, to go past (without any affect)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>мину́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">minútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миновать.html>минова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn (of age)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>ми́нуло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>со́рок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú <b>mínulo</b> sórok let.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He has turned forty.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>мину́ть</a></b> with the meaning "to pass (of time)" or "to go past" can have past stress either <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>ми́нул</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mínul</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>мину́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">minúl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whereas with the meaning "to turn (an age)" it can only have the past stress as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минуть.html>ми́нул</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mínul</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In either case the past active participle is only <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минувший.html>мину́вший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">minúvšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неминуемый.html>немину́емый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neminújemyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">немину́чий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neminúčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разминуться.html>размину́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razminútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:минувший.html>мину́вший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">minúvšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***мир.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a> (168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mirъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peace; world</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*MeyH-ró-s</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mitigate</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mir</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>миры́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>миро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> peace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>война́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vojná i <b>mir</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">war and <b>peace</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mir</b> vo vsjóm <b>míre</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">world <b>peace</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оплот.html>опло́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oplót <b>míra</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">stronghold <b>of peace</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>universe; world; planet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:происхождение.html>происхожде́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">proisxoždénije <b>míra</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">origin <b>of the universe</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">До Архимеда в Древней Греции самым большим числом считалось 10 000 000, т.е. 1000 <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">мириад</span> (<span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">мириадой</span> называлось число 10 000 от греческого слова «мириос» — «неисчислимо большое»). </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Всего в данном отрывке Ипполит приводит 13 чисел, относящихся к расстояниям между небесными телами. Расстояния исчисляются тысячами <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">мириад</span> стадий и даны с точностью до стадии. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:множественный.html>мно́жественном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числе́</a>">мн. ч.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:поэтический.html>поэти́ческое</a>">поэт.</span> бесчисленное количество, неисчислимое множество <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Ночь ложилась над городом, и вся необъятная, вспухшая от замёрзшего снега поляна Невы, с последним отблеском солнца, осыпалась бесконечными <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">мириадами</span> искр иглистого инея. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Да сыплет ночь своей бездонной урной // К нам <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">мириады</span> звёзд. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">В капителях колонн, когда погасало электричество, загорались <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">мириады</span> светляков, а в воздухе плыли болотные огни. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мириться.html>мири́ться</a> (10688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирить.html>мири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мириться.html>мири́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mirítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помириться.html>помири́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примириться.html>примири́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make peace <i>(with)</i>, to be reconciled <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помириться.html>помири́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomirítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to accept, to put up <i>(with)</i>, to reconcile oneself <i>(to)</i>, to resign oneself <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мириться.html>мири́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirítʹsja</b> so svoím položénijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to accept one's situation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мириться.html>мири́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишение.html>лише́ниями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirítʹsja</b> s lišénijami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put up with hardships; rough it</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мириться.html>мири́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirítʹsja</b> s nedostátkami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to condone shortcomings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мириться.html>мири́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nelʹzjá <b>mirítʹsja</b> s étim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this cannot be tolerated</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирить.html>мири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мировоззрение.html>мировоззре́ние</a> (9649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззрение.html>воззре́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozzrénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weltanschauung</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировоззрение.html>мировоззре́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mirovozzrénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировоззрение.html>мировоззре́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировоззрение.html>мировоззре́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировоззрение.html>мировоззре́ний</a></b>)

***мировой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a> (4869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mir</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">world; peace</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mirovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> world; global, worldwide
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:океан.html>океа́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Mirovój</b> okeán</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_Ocean" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:World Ocean"><b>World</b> Ocean</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirovóje</b> dérevo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/world_tree" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:world tree"><b>world</b> tree</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рекорд.html>реко́рд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirovój</b> rekórd</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>world</b> record</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рынок.html>ры́нок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirovój</b> rýnok</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>worldwide</b> market</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мировы́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́менем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>mirovým</b> ímenem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with a <b>worldwide</b> reputation, <b>world</b>-famous</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всемирный.html>всеми́рный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vsemírnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вселенский.html>вселе́нский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vselénskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">общемирово́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obščemirovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> first-rate, first-class, great
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парень.html>па́рень</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>mirovój</b> párenʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is a <b>first-class</b> guy</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наилучший.html>наилу́чший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nailúčšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличный.html>отли́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otlíčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прекрасный.html>прекра́сный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prekrásnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:классный.html>кла́ссный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">klássnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resolved by settlement rather than trial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirovóje</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">case resolved through a settlement</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> petty <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">related to minor civil and criminal cases</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mirovój</b> sud</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>petty</b> court</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mirovój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мирово́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мировы́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мировой.html>мировы́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> petty-court judge <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">judge who deals with minor civil and criminal cases</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирок.html>миро́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mirók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирок.html>мирка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирок.html>мирки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мирок.html>мирко́в</a></b>)
</p>

Štóby ovladétʹ jevó vnimánijem i soznánijem, nedostátočno podtasóvyvatʹsja pod jevó jazýk, no núžno tákže umétʹ i mýslitʹ na jevó manér. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>”</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"He has his own train of thought!" thought the prosecutor. ***миролюбивый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:миролюбивый.html>миролюби́вый</a> (10551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:миролюбивый.html>миролюби́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">miroljubívyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>peaceful, peaceable, peace-loving</li></ol>

***мисс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мисс.html>мисс</a> (7668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Miss</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мисс.html>мисс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">miss</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
